84	            Retrieves a namespace from the dictionary with a specific version number
85	
86	            Example:
87	            --------
88	
89	            >>> from owslib.namespaces import Namespaces
90	            >>> ns = Namespaces()

93	            >>> ns.get_versioned_namespace('ows','1.1.0')

95	        """
96	
97	        if ver is None:

103	            version += s
